  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

  <span id="freeText11893622611154800949" style="display:none">After Reading: Review to come!!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />OMG!! If has a cover!! Finally! And I love it!!!!<br /><br /><br />Okay according to JLA:<br /><br />- "DB" was left behind in Vegas in Origin. But he may make an appearance again.<br />- Archer and Dee are together in Opposition.<br />- Blake is really dead. Like, dead dead dead.<br />- What would be the mix between an Origin and Luxen? A: pretty badass<br />- You will find out in Opposition why Daemon didn’t reply to Katy in the end<br />- Katy’s mom will be back for Opposition<br />- *Spoiler for Opposition* The Luxen that invaded Earth, have never been around people before.<br />- Obsession sets up Opposition.<br />- Some Origins escaped during the diversion.<br />- Hunter and his brothers will be in Opposition.<br />- Daemon and Katy will NOT have a baby in Opposition. So here is the quote I found: <br /><br />“Katy<br /><br />I always had this plan for the off chance I was around for the end of the world. I’d climb up on my roof top, turn up the radio, blast R.E.M.’s It’s The End of The World, and watch it all go down from my lofty perch.<br /><br />Except real life rarely turned out that cool.<br /><br />And it was really happening—it was the end of the world as we knew it, and I sure as hell didn’t feel fine.<br /><br />Everything had changed and we had been the catalyst for it all.” <br /><br /><br />I had one of the happiest moments of my life when I found out that the fifth book was going to be in Katy's and Daemon's POV and that it already had a title. I was dancing around in joy, but then my eyes fell on the date 2014 and I felt like ripping someone's throat out. Okay maybe not that extreme but I still really wanted to punch something. 2014 is so far and I so want the book right now. Origin had an awful cliffhanger which left me confused and depressed. I thought the cliffhanger for Opal was bad but Origin was completely and totally awful. Actually awful is too good of a word for it. I really want this book to come out faster. In other words I need this book NOW!!!!!! I really need more of Daemon and Katy.</span>

<div id="review_575744718" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/575744718" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/575744718?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer575744718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13805563495005093728"><b>4.5 Save the World stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b1643796-db2e-4b95-8c74-ce4e669637df_zps333479c6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407403446i/10709061.jpg' alt=' photo b1643796-db2e-4b95-8c74-ce4e669637df_zps333479c6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is one of those epically awesome series. There is just no other way to describe it. When I first picked up <i>Obsidian</i>, I had no idea what to expect. I read paranormal ya every now and then, but it’s not my genre of choice. Still, I gave it a go. I was hooked. I loved everything about Daemon and Katy. All 5 of these books were captivating and hilarious reads full of action, humor, suspense and love. <br/><br/>Opposition starts off right where Origin left off… Daemon, Katy an</span>
  <span id="freeText13805563495005093728" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Save the World stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/b1643796-db2e-4b95-8c74-ce4e669637df_zps333479c6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407403446i/10709061.jpg" alt=" photo b1643796-db2e-4b95-8c74-ce4e669637df_zps333479c6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is one of those epically awesome series. There is just no other way to describe it. When I first picked up <i>Obsidian</i>, I had no idea what to expect. I read paranormal ya every now and then, but it’s not my genre of choice. Still, I gave it a go. I was hooked. I loved everything about Daemon and Katy. All 5 of these books were captivating and hilarious reads full of action, humor, suspense and love. <br><br>Opposition starts off right where Origin left off… Daemon, Katy and friends trying to save the world thats been invaded. Who can they trust? Those they thought would never betray them have gone to the dark side, and those that have always been enemies have now come to their aide. It’s a hot mess. Through it all, Katy and Daemon have each other. Daemon’s love will never change.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/4a111281-da93-4b94-ab0c-bc8b109c0d4e_zps02ac8a3f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407403446i/10709062.jpg" alt=" photo 4a111281-da93-4b94-ab0c-bc8b109c0d4e_zps02ac8a3f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Daemon and his Kitten have to be one of my favorite book couples ever. They have the best back and fourth banter. Both of them are so funny, but really sweet and romantic too. Daemon Black. Oh sweet alien babies I love him! He is one of my favorite ya book boyfriends. Every time I hear him say Kitten, I melt. I love the way he loves Katy. He thinks the world of her and he’s not afraid to show it. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’ve got a big heart, Kitten. That’s what I love about you most. Well, that and I am a really big fan of your sweet body, but your heart? Yeah, that completes the package of you, wraps it up with a nice little bow. It makes you perfect to me.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/23d2456a-fc55-4178-9e55-55814fbd5631_zpsa87d0c0f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407403446i/10709063.jpg" alt=" photo 23d2456a-fc55-4178-9e55-55814fbd5631_zpsa87d0c0f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s not just the main characters I love, there are quite a few secondary characters that are equally amazing! I really love Archer! And of course Dee and Dawson. <br><br>This review is going to be much shorter than normal for me, because this is a story you don’t want to have spoiled. Not even a little bit. There are so many awesome twists and turns. I was on the edge of my seat most of the book. I laughed a lot, I even cried some. I’m feeling a little sad that this series has come to an end. I’m really going to miss Daemon Black and Kat. <br><br>If you haven’t read this series yet, all 5 books are out so now you have no excuse. It is my #1 paranormal ya series. Daemon Black is unforgettable and Katy is an awesome book nerd. Their love is something special and this series is just fantastic! Do yourself a favor and pick them up! ♥<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/902f003f-d4ed-419f-8977-0572a361cce9_zps6f7dd7df.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407403446i/10709064.jpg" alt=" photo 902f003f-d4ed-419f-8977-0572a361cce9_zps6f7dd7df.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>We were together. It didn’t matter how many hours, days, months or years we had stretched out in front of us; we’d always be together. This kind of love was the real deal.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/GIFS/DAEMONGIF_zpsa9adfc3b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407226564ra/10658448.gif" alt=" photo DAEMONGIF_zpsa9adfc3b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer9188249900613668271"><b>
  <blockquote>Back in the day, I had this plan for the off chance that I was around for the whole end-of-the-world thing. It involved climbing up on my roof and blasting R.E.M.'s "It's the End of the World as We Know it (And I Feel Fine)" as loud as humanly possible, but real life rarely turns out that cool.<br/><br/>It was happening-everything about the world as we knew it was ending, and it sure as hell did not feel fine. Or Cool.</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>The Luxen invasion happened. =( <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519575302ra/25121452.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>and things changed for everyone. <br/><br/>People were being k</span>
  <span id="freeText9188249900613668271" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>Back in the day, I had this plan for the off chance that I was around for the whole end-of-the-world thing. It involved climbing up on my roof and blasting R.E.M.'s "It's the End of the World as We Know it (And I Feel Fine)" as loud as humanly possible, but real life rarely turns out that cool.<br><br>It was happening-everything about the world as we knew it was ending, and it sure as hell did not feel fine. Or Cool.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The Luxen invasion happened. =( <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519575302ra/25121452.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and things changed for everyone. <br><br>People were being killed left and right. Daemon, Dawson and Dee were taken away to go with the leader. Katy, Archer and Beth were left to try to stay alive. <br><br>But Daemon made his way back. They all eventually did. Took Dee awhile as she was brainwashed the most. <br><br>And there were still some funny tidbits in the book. I love when a book can throw in some funny moments. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Archer sighed like a petulant teenager stuck in a car for too long. There was a beat of silence. "Are we there yet?"<br><br>Daemon groaned. "I'm going to sew your damn lips together."<br><br>********<br><br>Well, shit balls for dinner on Sunday.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I'm going to have to remember and use that last one =) <br><br>And lo and behold, they team up with some of the enemy alien friends, the Arum. I love Hunter, he was my favorite Arum. Their leader was a crackpot =D <br><br>We have some show downs with the alien races and the human mutants. Some people get killed that made me sad. <br><br>But the ending made me so happy. Everyone together that mattered for the most part. And a new edition, Ashley. That's all I'm saying party people. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510921561ra/24467439.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Happy Reading! <br><br>Mel ♥<br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2018/02/lux-opposition-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a><br><br>AMAZON: <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/review/R3ORAV70JCNCN?ref_=glimp_1rv_cl" rel="nofollow noopener">TINY REVIEW</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1131408170?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1131408170" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18167733635745842935"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I'm game for anything with you, Daemon Black.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>That's it.The series that made me put aside my truest love after books (that would be sleep),that occupied my every thought for a week,that <b>made me an antisocial madwoman mumbling about aliens</b>,is over.Kat and Daemon's story is over.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390409423ra/8207993.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It didn't matter how many hours,days,months,or years we had stretched out in front of us;we'd always be together.This kind of love was the real deal,stronger than a whole planet full of psycho aliens </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText18167733635745842935" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I'm game for anything with you, Daemon Black.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>That's it.The series that made me put aside my truest love after books (that would be sleep),that occupied my every thought for a week,that <b>made me an antisocial madwoman mumbling about aliens</b>,is over.Kat and Daemon's story is over.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390409423ra/8207993.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It didn't matter how many hours,days,months,or years we had stretched out in front of us;we'd always be together.This kind of love was the real deal,stronger than a whole planet full of psycho aliens and an entire government.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh,holy llama drama,it hurts.Kat,Daemon,Dee,Archer,Dawson,Luc,they were my friends,my companions,I felt with them and fought and cried and loved.From Petersburg and Area 51 to Las Vegas and the Arum lair,I was with them,followed them as their story unfolded,from the first moment Kat met Daemon in her My Blog is better than your Vlog shirt to the alien invasion and the inevitable and heartbreaking choices they had to make.<b>They're family.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441452328ra/16111803.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I started reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a>,I thought it would be another paranormal love story,but I was wrong.It was so much more.As the plot thickened and the tension increased,as unexpected deaths occured and Kat and Deamon proved again and again how much they love each other,I found a safe haven,a shelter from reality.And while their story had painful and infuriating and frustrating moments,it was <b>beautiful</b>.<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13644055.Shadows___Opposition__Lux__0_5___5_" title="Shadows / Opposition (Lux #0.5, #5) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Opposition</a> felt like I was watching a <b>badass science fiction movie</b> with the Earth in the verge of Apocalypse and the good guys working with their enemies in order to survive and save mankind from enslavement and extinction.Relationships were tested,unholy alliances were forged and the events that started when Dawson fell in love with a human reached their crescendo with Kat and Deamon's <b>otherwordly and wonderful love</b>.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Everything had changed and we had been the catalyst for it all.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I absolutely recommend this series to everyone who enjoys romance with paranormal elements and kickass battles,and I hope you will love Lux as much as I did!</span>
  <a data-text-id="18167733635745842935" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/971404000?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer971404000" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5468121026598793144"><b>5–HEART-POUNDING, INTENSE, AND AMAZING–Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520279153i/25166873._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I can't think of the last time a book had me sitting on the edge of my seat, biting my nails, and holding my breath. <i>Opposition</i> captivated and enthralled me from the first heart-pounding page to the last. I LOVED IT! </b><br/><br/>I am so sad to see this series eqnd. I have LOVED watching Katy's and Daemon's characters grow and mature over the course of the books. <br/><br/>Katy began this series as a lovable and strong character who was obstinate, and sometimes even pigheade</span>
  <span id="freeText5468121026598793144" style="display:none"><b>5–HEART-POUNDING, INTENSE, AND AMAZING–Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520279153i/25166873._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I can't think of the last time a book had me sitting on the edge of my seat, biting my nails, and holding my breath. <i>Opposition</i> captivated and enthralled me from the first heart-pounding page to the last. I LOVED IT! </b><br><br>I am so sad to see this series eqnd. I have LOVED watching Katy's and Daemon's characters grow and mature over the course of the books. <br><br>Katy began this series as a lovable and strong character who was obstinate, and sometimes even pigheaded. By the final book, she'd grown into a stronger, more lovable, admirable, resilient, and courageous version of herself. She ended up one of the best YA female leads I've read to date. <br><br>As for Daemon, well, he'll <b>always</b> be his arrogant, lovable, sarcastic, loyal, charming, and egoistical self. But he's also not the same stubborn, human-snubbing boy who first opened his door to Katy and treated her so horribly. He grew into a man that acknowledged some of his beliefs were wrong and PROVED he would do ANYTHING for the woman he loved. <br><br>For me, the area I felt Katy and Daemon grew the most was in their gradual realization that they were stronger together than apart. By the fourth book they were a solid team and knew their greatest strength and power was in relying on each other. Their complex and awesome relationship was what I loved the most about the Lux series. <br><br>I can't end my review without expressing how grateful I am I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14060046.Obsession" title="Obsession by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsession</a>, an adult spinoff of this series. Had I not read <i>Obsession</i>, I would have never pick up <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a>, the first book in the Lux series, and I would have forever missed out on an amazing Young Adult read. <br><br><b>I can wholeheartedly say that I have loved every single second I've spend with Daemon, Katy and the rest of the motley cast of characters. It's always bittersweet to say goodbye to a much loved series, especially one that will forever hold a piece of my heart. </b><br><br><b>Side Note: </b>As a THANK YOU for Opposition hitting the USA Today Bestseller’s list at number 34 and put the Lux Series on the New York Times YA Series list at number 4 this week, Jennifer Armentrout gave us a taste of Daemon and Kat, a few years after Opposition. I couldn't stop smiling while reading it. <br><br>Enjoy! <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/a-special-thank-you/">http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/a-s...</a></span>

<div id="review_1017331043" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1017331043" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1017331043?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20753858-opposition">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=para-dystopian-sci-fi-fantasy">para-dystopian-sci-fi-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1017331043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4444249513444610749">I helped save the planet in this book so… you’re welcome. It was my pleasure to save all of mankind alongside one of my absolute favorite book couples, Daemon Black and Katy Swartz.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"They're up to something big. "Obviously." I smiled faintly. "The whole invading-Earth part kind of gave that away."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391056919ra/8324643.gif' width='390' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I never thought I would fall as hard as I did for these characters when I gave the first book of this series a chance. I mean a book about aliens in high school? But it happened and I loved every pag</span>
  <span id="freeText4444249513444610749" style="display:none">I helped save the planet in this book so… you’re welcome. It was my pleasure to save all of mankind alongside one of my absolute favorite book couples, Daemon Black and Katy Swartz.<br><br><b>
  <i>"They're up to something big. "Obviously." I smiled faintly. "The whole invading-Earth part kind of gave that away."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391056919ra/8324643.gif" width="390" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I never thought I would fall as hard as I did for these characters when I gave the first book of this series a chance. I mean a book about aliens in high school? But it happened and I loved every page of this series, every sarcastic comment by Daemon, every loving word shared between Daemon and Katy and the many other characters that will be just as sorely missed.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407332060i/10676128._SY540_.jpg" width="390" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Daemon and Katy are the perfect book couple that would definitely light up the silver screen if given the opportunity. They face the end of the world, they make alliances with the unexpected and their bond just gets stronger.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407332814i/10676339._SY540_.jpg" width="390" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Even if you’re not a fan of paranormal or young adult genres give this series a shot. Jennifer Armentrout thank you for the laughs, the love, the electric kisses, the nonstop action and the possibilities of the unknown that were written so wonderfully that all the scenes were so vivid and bright!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407331549i/10676048.gif" width="320" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...I'll try but I sure would love to see this series made into a movie! </span>
  <a data-text-id="4444249513444610749" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I enjoyed banters (it is Daemon after all) but overall I didn't like this book because it didn't reached the level of awesomeness from previous instalments.<br><blockquote>__________________________________</blockquote><br>PRE-REVIEW:<br><br>I NEED THIS BOOK LIKE NOW!     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1693157779" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1693157779" />
    <a title="elena" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/51318038-elena"><img alt="elena" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605725028p2/51318038.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1693157779?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="elena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="elena" href="/user/show/51318038-elena">elena</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1693157779" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13428579846392050595"><blockquote>
  <i>❝Kat fascinated me, every aspect of her. She was beautiful, but it went so beyond that. She was so incredibly strong, and she bore the scars of her strength like a prizefighter. She was smart and stubborn, but most of all, she was kind, and she'd given me the ultimate gift when she loved me in return.❞</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Thank you Jennifer L. Armentrout</b> for letting me find a way to love one of your series and persuade me to keep going when I didn't mean to and expected to completely fall in love with it and com</span>
  <span id="freeText13428579846392050595" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>❝Kat fascinated me, every aspect of her. She was beautiful, but it went so beyond that. She was so incredibly strong, and she bore the scars of her strength like a prizefighter. She was smart and stubborn, but most of all, she was kind, and she'd given me the ultimate gift when she loved me in return.❞</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Thank you Jennifer L. Armentrout</b> for letting me find a way to love one of your series and persuade me to keep going when I didn't mean to and expected to completely fall in love with it and completely shut down everything around me just to see where the next journey of Daemon and Katy would go. I never thought about loving <i>Paranormal Romance</i> at least a bit and little did I know that this series would be the first one I would completely fall in love with and miss it over and over again as I finished one book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454702745i/18003021._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>Love was a gift.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Opposition</i> was no different than <i>Origin and Opal.</i> Katy and Daemon are trying to find a way to be together, stay together and just survive and stop all this Luxen mess. But in Opposition, nothing is the same. I mean, Katy is a <b>badass</b> and Daemon just falls in love with her over and over and even more when he sees her make some bitch ass Lux bleed. It's funny how it all went from hating each other to taking a bullet for each other and finding ways to prove their love for each other over and over, but I guess it was worth waiting and worth reading until finding out truths and all.<br><br><b>Katy</b> once again is a freaking badass and still that book nerd. After finally being able to stop this mess and finally be with Daemon for as long as she can, she's back to book blogging and fangirling over books and talking about them non-stop, remembering covers and using quotes as cheesy comebacks. She grew a shit ton more becoming stronger and stronger as she was able to fight with the power she was given, now that she knows how it works and what is really is. She was fierce and a savage at times, not caring what others had to say and completely was able to defend herself like she's been doing since book 1. She's been positive and kept her head up when the bad times came along and didn't really let anything or anyone stop her or get in her way. I loved seeing her character development grow in a way I never expected and I love the person she became. She accepted the person she became and wasn't a complete whining bitch, not caring about anything or anyone but instead cared about everyone, wanted to make sure everything was okay and didn't give up on finding out reasons behind her power and strength.<br><br><b>Daemon</b> again is the same sweet, loving, caring, yet stupid angel who cares so much about his love, Katy. He's grown into someone who decided to take a bullet for the girl, made sure she was okay and happy, and would do anything to make her happy and keep her safe. He hasn't been an asshole to Katy since Origin and all of that was completely refreshing, not expecting any of the respectful mind he carries with her and respectful manners of him towards her. He was the same douche and jerk to others but when it came to Katy, he was always different and everything about him changed; softened. He was still the strong leader and would keep leading his family and friends, finding out how to stop this and finding out who was and is behind everything, not leaving anyone behind or anything. He was always finding ways to make everything work and everything about him was about the Daemon I fell in love with and boy am I glad I did! His relationship with Katy wasn't rushed and he never rushed anything, never forced her into anything but instead took his time with her and made sure she was okay with everything happening. He was still the protective brother when it came to Dee and Dawson, and when it came to Katy, he was still the boyfriend who would send one of his own kind flying because he has touched the girl's neck in front of him and well, I don't think a girls boyfriend would allow that anyway.<br><br><b>Dee</b> was completely a bitch in the beginning and everything about her faded and left me upset. Of course there was a reason and it wasn't really her controlling herself, it wasn't her doing all that damage and it wasn't her trying to kill Katy, but she was still rude and arrogant at times. It's like she and Daemon switched personalities from the first book and Daemon was Dee while Dee was Daemon. It was sad and left me a little broken because I've loved Dee since the beginning and even though she's had to go through so much shit and been put through a lot, I still wished she was able to pretend like her brother while trying to save and defend Katy but it was like she didn't put much effort to it or didn't even bother trying. I'm glad everything went back to normal and her and Katy are back to being best friends, sisters now and putting everything in their spot, like it used to be. They've both left the horrible and heartbreaking past behind and decided to take a step forward and see how that would work and turn out.<br><br><b>Archer</b> is completely in love with Dee and he just didn't bother trying to hide it. He didn't care about Daemon being the brother and even when he knew who Dee could be and become, how she could act and how hard she can hit, he would also have a soft spot for her and I was glad he was the protective one as well. I loved him in Origin and I loved him in Opposition as well. Nothing about him was wrong, he wasn't annoying, and he didn't end up betraying the people he promised to help and not leave behind. He was different than everyone and by different I mean he's <i>different.</i> He isn't just a Lux and isn't just able to shoot a powerful and bright light from his palm but is able to read minds as well without wanting to at times. Oh the moments of him and Katy when he was inside her head. God I wonder where their friendship went after.<br><br><b>Luc</b> is the same hilarious kid and I can't say much about him. He was mentioned and even though he is a favorite of many, he wasn't my favorite. Archer was my favorite while Luc was a typical side character that I didn't pay much attention to. He had his hilarious comebacks and was the witty kid who made me giggle because of how he acted and was around others. He was strong, despite his size and age, and was also one who didn't end up betraying them. I had small doubts about him, thinking he would end up like Blake and would ditch Katy, Daemon and the rest and go wander and do whatever pleases him. He sort of did, but because he's a kid, he's different. He came back in the end and I was glad he did, again with his stupid yet adorable lines.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454702745i/18003021._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>Kat whipped toward me, her eyes glowing from within. In that moment, she looked like a goddess—a goddess of vengeance.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Again, <i>Opposition</i> was quite similar to the rest. It kept dealing with the Luxen and Arum and finding out how to put an end to it all. Since this is the 5th and final installment of the series, there was an end to it and Daemon and Katy finally were able to stay together, with nothing to worry and leave the past behind, looking for the future. JLA has definitely convinced me into reading her other books and now I am convinced she will be able to make me love them. Even if I don't like the first novel, I'll probably end up liking or loving the 2nd and the rest and just completely fall in love with her phenomenal writing again. <br><br>Katy and Daemon had me wanting more of them together and I missed them constantly, not having finished the series. Now that I'm done, I don't know what other couple I will love so much and will be just as loving and beautiful as this one. They were both perfect for each other and I thank Jennifer for creating such a perfect pair that always had me smiling, wishing there was a Daemon in my life. Now, who knows what fictional couple will "replace" Katy and Daemon and will have me bawling my eyes out because of how cute they are around each other, together, and even around others. <i>Oh man I love them both so much how is this possible?!?</i><br><br>There's so much more to this one. Ass kicking, family sacrificing each other, heartbreaking moments, and moments that had me wanting more and not wanting to stop reading the lines because of how beatifully written it was. Now, I guess it's my time to say goodbye to this alien-mojo world and the world where a jerk face ended up having me fall head over toes for him because of how he would be, acted and how much he really decided to change just for a girl. It's my time to say goodbye to a girl who was like me in such little fractures who loves books and would spend her time reading and gushing over covers and fictional characters. Little did I know I would want to be saying goodbye to a world where aliens exist and fight each others kind to protect other kind because of the connections they feel towards them. Strong and real connections, unlike the ones they never felt before.<br><br>Of course there are many other characters who were introduced, only leaving me hating them and wishing they were thrown into a cliff and would completely shatter and bleed. <i>Oh wait...</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454702745i/18003021._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>“That was for being a complete bitch!” She caught Sadi in the back, pushing her forward. “And this is for even thinking it was okay to touch me.” The final swing came from the front, snapping Sadi's head into next week. “And that is for even speaking Daemon's name.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm just surprised this series completely caught my heart because of how everything worked out and how everything came to an end. It was a conclusion, and I can't say it was the best, it was just a lot more action packed and was the one that had me laughing, grinning and smiling so much because of the threats and actions taken, but <i>Origin</i> will definitely have to be my favorite and will remain as my favorite.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13428579846392050595" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2416139552" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16761836725753794157"><b>
  <i>It's the End of the World as We Know It (And I Feel Fine)</i>
</b><br/><br/>Yes, the world has beyond doubt changed<br/>BUT<br/>Katy does NOT feel fine.<br/><br/>Daimon has picked a side and abandoned her.<br/>Or this is what Katy thinks.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>“Kat.” He uttered my name like it was some kind of prayer, and then he pressed a kiss against the skin behind my ear. “I broke every rule of my kind to heal you and keep you with me. I … burned down an entire city to keep you safe. I’ve killed for you. Did you think I’d forget what you mean to me? </b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText16761836725753794157" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>It's the End of the World as We Know It (And I Feel Fine)</i>
</b><br /><br />Yes, the world has beyond doubt changed<br />BUT<br />Katy does NOT feel fine.<br /><br />Daimon has picked a side and abandoned her.<br />Or this is what Katy thinks.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Kat.” He uttered my name like it was some kind of prayer, and then he pressed a kiss against the skin behind my ear. “I broke every rule of my kind to heal you and keep you with me. I … burned down an entire city to keep you safe. I’ve killed for you. Did you think I’d forget what you mean to me? That anything in this world— in any world— would be stronger than my love for you?”</b>
</i><br /><br />Deep sigh...<br /><br />Soon, there will be a reunion. It won't be a happy reunion.<br /><br />Daemon is stressed, scared for Katy and he tries unsuccessfully to look evil.<br />Dawson is stressed, scared for pregnant Beth and he tries unsuccessfully to look evil also.<br />Dee is peaceful, content and she looks evil successfully.<br /><br />All hell will break lose in Las Vegas and before Daemon and Katy realise what they have done, they will be out of the frying pan into the fire and now human soldiers will be their new guards.<br /><br />And before they can mumble “Luc what are you doing with Nancy?”, it is about time for them to meet the Arum and their psycho leader Lotho. By the way his comparison to Loki, I thought it was just brilliant!<br /><br />Who are finally the bad guys?<br />The Luxen?<br />The humans?<br />The Arum?<br /><br />And moreover:<br />Who is human?<br />Who is Luxen?<br />Who is Origin?<br /><br />You cannot really tell. <br />All around a post-apocalyptic scenario plays out and the only thing missing are the zombies. <br />Thankfully and strangely, you can still find toilet paper at the supermarket.<br /><br />This is an amazing book that it could be easily a Hollywood’s blockbuster film or a successful TV series. <br />I had such fun with this series and I would really love more books from this world.<br /><br />Previous books:<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2226951170?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1%20" rel="nofollow noopener">Review Obsidian (Lux, #1)</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2235915845?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Review Onyx (Lux, #2)</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2396078451?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Review Opal (Lux, #3)</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2410754583?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Review Origin (Lux, #4)</a></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer820245415" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5552026510955393403">I FINALLY finished this series! While I didn't enjoy this last book at all compared to the first one in the series, I will always love Katy and Daemon as characters. This series could been much more effective as a trilogy and I love/hate all the Twilight parallels (I really can't decide if they are genius or obnoxious). I think the story got too big for the world ultimately but I am glad I stuck with it and finished it. Jennifer's writing is addictive and hilarious as always and I'm excited to v</span>
  <span id="freeText5552026510955393403" style="display:none">I FINALLY finished this series! While I didn't enjoy this last book at all compared to the first one in the series, I will always love Katy and Daemon as characters. This series could been much more effective as a trilogy and I love/hate all the Twilight parallels (I really can't decide if they are genius or obnoxious). I think the story got too big for the world ultimately but I am glad I stuck with it and finished it. Jennifer's writing is addictive and hilarious as always and I'm excited to venture off into some of her other work!</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3150333683" />
    <a title="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books"><img alt="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582051737p2/6245313.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3150333683?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" href="/user/show/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books">❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=feels-book">feels-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=non-arc">non-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=recommend-read">recommend-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=2020-read">2020-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3150333683" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8625452733811762339"><a href='https://ibb.co/85JM39J' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579555383i/28812686._SX540_.jpg' alt='2' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>'OPPOSITION'</b> is the fifth and final book in Jennifer L. Armentrout's 'Lux' series. It picks up where the previous book left off.<br/><br/>What a bittersweet feeling when I closed out of that last page. I was happy with the ending, all my favourite characters survived but I was sad that I had to say goodbye. I feel like they are a part of me, I've been reading this series back to back loving every single moment of it. The heartache, the losses, the love, the angst, the tears, so many feels, so many tim</span>
  <span id="freeText8625452733811762339" style="display:none"><a href="https://ibb.co/85JM39J" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579555383i/28812686._SX540_.jpg" alt="2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>'OPPOSITION'</b> is the fifth and final book in Jennifer L. Armentrout's 'Lux' series. It picks up where the previous book left off.<br><br>What a bittersweet feeling when I closed out of that last page. I was happy with the ending, all my favourite characters survived but I was sad that I had to say goodbye. I feel like they are a part of me, I've been reading this series back to back loving every single moment of it. The heartache, the losses, the love, the angst, the tears, so many feels, so many times my heart literally stopped beating. A whirlwind of emotions. <br><br>And god I loved Archer!! His mind reading, the back and forth jabs between him and Daemon. My most favorite book characters to date!! <br><br>I can finally and honestly say that I now have 5 PNR books behind me and I'm just going to keep increasing that number!!<br><br>Thank you to ALL the people who recommended this series to me!! It only took me like years and months to get to it!! But I am so glad I pulled up those big girl panties and jumped on this all in the name of challenging myself!! Yet again I am so thankful I took the plunge!!<br><br>5 for 5!! 5 Books/each with 5 stars!! Unheard of!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <div></div>
  <div>
    <a href="https://katfenton.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1564780031i/27930520.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_374362007" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/374362007" />
    <a title="Andreea Pop" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop"><img alt="Andreea Pop" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486663526p2/4858513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/374362007?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andreea Pop" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andreea Pop" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop">Andreea Pop</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=creepy-abilities">creepy-abilities</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=epic-battles">epic-battles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=awesome-romance">awesome-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=amazing-feelings">amazing-feelings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=good-vs-bad">good-vs-bad</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer374362007" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11553506553186528519"><b>REVIEW:</b><br/><br/><a href='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-bZefb5OlnGI/U-NOYrPuE8I/AAAAAAAAOGY/MkFm_gMVAQE/s1600/10341351.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709632.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I’m bawling my eyes right at this very moment, because this series is over and lemme just tell you that it ended <b>PERFECTLY</b>. <i>Opposition</i> is absolutely top-notch fangirling material, set to conclude one of the most addictive stories by raising the bar on sexiness, action, heartbreak and pure, unloaded fun. It was everything I could’ve hoped for and then some – I completely loved it.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>“Kitten?”<br/>“Yeah?”<br/>His eyes were beautiful when they met mine, luminous and clear, and a long moment stretc</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText11553506553186528519" style="display:none"><b>REVIEW:</b><br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-bZefb5OlnGI/U-NOYrPuE8I/AAAAAAAAOGY/MkFm_gMVAQE/s1600/10341351.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709632.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m bawling my eyes right at this very moment, because this series is over and lemme just tell you that it ended <b>PERFECTLY</b>. <i>Opposition</i> is absolutely top-notch fangirling material, set to conclude one of the most addictive stories by raising the bar on sexiness, action, heartbreak and pure, unloaded fun. It was everything I could’ve hoped for and then some – I completely loved it.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Kitten?”<br>“Yeah?”<br>His eyes were beautiful when they met mine, luminous and clear, and a long moment stretched out between us. “I love you.”</b>
</i><br><br>At the end of <i>Origin</i>, we could see that things were going south pretty quickly. But the “little” stunts our favorite gang pulled in the last book are in no way at the scale of epicness from this one, because shit just hit the fan in <i>Opposition</i>. World domination. Alien invasion. Dystopia setting. Apocalypse loading. You know, the usual holy shit stuff. <br><br>One of the reasons this series is so worth reading is the characters. Intense, realistic, strong characters. Katy Swarz, ex-book blogger extraordinaire and current alien hybrid with serious mojo, is a tough chick that you can't help than admire. Stubborn, kind, determined and definitely badass, I loved that she still found the power to simply smile and joke in the midst of all that's going on. She proved countless times that she's a selfless, caring person that would do anything to protect the ones she loves and that kind of strength is always awe-inspiring. She's had to go through some awful stuff and now she fights to end it all and make herself a future. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SEiWIQVULZA/U-NObCxfMQI/AAAAAAAAOG0/5Zw4rF1DRz8/s1600/poz%C2%A6%C3%A2+22.JPG" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407405946i/10709634._SY540_.jpg" height="320" width="213" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Daemon Black is still the king of swoons, sarcasm-dripping lines and alpha-male behavior. The magnitude of his feelings for Katy is unbelievable and I had to remind myself that he's just fictional, because otherwise I would order a Daemon Black right at my doorstep. Oh, and he brings out the big guns on smoking hotness that will have you blush in a can't-get-that-goofy-smile-off-my-face kind of way. And the romantic declarations will swoop you off your feet, cause they're at a whole new level. The same alien eye candy with very mischievous thoughts and horribly arrogant attitude, only this time he's all grown up. Watch out, cause you're about to love him even more (if that's even possible). <br><br><i>
  <b>“I broke every rule of my kind to heal you and keep you with me. I married you and burned down an entire city to keep you safe. I’ve killed for you. Did you think I’d forget what you mean to me? That anything in this world—in any world—would be stronger than my love for you?”</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ERkzMmnQe3I/U-NOZjdh5fI/AAAAAAAAOGs/4CQ2E2TaO4Y/s1600/poz%C2%A6%C3%A2+3.JPG" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407405946i/10709633.jpg" height="238" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Katy and Daemon are a sizzling pair. Their romance will have your heart singing sappy songs only because you cannot picture them apart. They're intense and completely crazy about each other. Lovestruck. And the best thing is that they make one another better, always ready to fight whatever life throws their way if they're in it together. Awww, I just love them. <i>*happy sigh*</i> <br><br><i>
  <b>“I had it with Daemon, but I wondered if we looked as love-struck as they did.<br>“You do,” Archer commented softly.<br>Ah, well, that was kind of embarrassing.<br>“Yes, it is,” he added.</b>
</i><br><br>Now I need to make a confession. Since Daemon has to be with Katy because they're so perfect together -- not that I would say no to his alien hotness -- I have to state, loud and clear, that freaking Archer is mine to the hell and back, lol. When I remember that we've only met him in the fourth book and that he's only a secondary character -- granted, a pretty important one -- the fact that my love for him knows no bounds shocks me every time. He's compassionate, realistic, deadly and smoking hot. Not to mention down-right hilarious. His bickering with Daemon cracked me up, but you could see they are on their way to becoming good and close friends. Just imagine: smartass comments to the millionth power. Katy actually said it best: <br><br><i>
  <b>“You know what I think?” She lowered her voice as if she were sharing a secret. “I think you do like Archer, and you just don’t want to admit that you’re in the beginning stages of a bromance to end all bromances.”</b>
</i><br><br>And seriously now, I love anyone who can make Daemon jealous over such trivial things like a hug or a candy bar. <i>*giggles*</i><br><br><i>
  <b>“I stood where I was, telling myself that the ugly heat invading my veins was indigestion and not jealousy. Totally not that, because Archer had nothing on me.<br>But did he need to hug her that long? And that hard? Come the hell on."</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Br_GJF7MmuQ/U-NOaY9lRUI/AAAAAAAAOG4/LlVO5hyJj9U/s1600/poz%C2%A6%C3%A2+11.JPG" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407405946i/10709635._SY540_.jpg" height="320" width="228" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But there's no worry regarding a possible Katy + Archer outcome, maybe only a wonderful friendship, because the guy is completely smitten with Dee. Romance overload, show me what you've got. These two are just totes adorbs together. <br><br><i>
  <b>“I wonder if I can get Dee to make me some,” Archer replied casually, ignoring Daemon. “You know, when she’s not on Team Kill Everyone.”<br>“She won’t make you any chicken,” Daemon retorted.<br>“Oh, she’ll make me fried chicken.” Archer laughed deeply. “She’ll make me all the chicken I want.”</b>
</i><br><br>Speaking of Dee, she was in a bad place most of this book and I was deeply hurt to see how it affected her once it all came crashing down. But she's still her sweet, kind and all-around great self and I'm glad she has Archer to protect and spoil her. <br><br>I looooved Luc. The kid is weird, but good-weird. Sure, he can be creepy and scary when he wants to be, but when he's all rainbows and sunshine? Overwhelmingly cute. Although what saddened me most was how lonely he truly was. I wished Katy just hugged the heck outta him once in a while, because being freakishly intelligent and a powerful mastermind must be exhausting at some point. But he's awesome and funny like no other and I'm glad he got accepted into the crew just like another family member. <br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-dPbTQVcuYmw/U-NOciCOsII/AAAAAAAAOHI/VNvVkNb7oDI/s1600/tumblr_inline_mmcxts9bEh1qz4rgp.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709636.gif" height="166" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Dawson &amp; Beth are still very much in the picture, thank the gods since I couldn't have handled any other deaths. I missed them a bit, especially Dawson, but they got their own little problem to worry about so I was okay with knowing they're safe and sound somewhere far away from the heat of the fight. <br><br>A shocking turn of events had us meeting up with Hunter, Serena and Lore and I was more than happy to catch up with them for a bit. Unlikely allies, but in the end a strong proof that Arum and Luxen could be, you know… friends. <br><br><i>
  <b>“Here?” Archer asked.<br>He nodded with a tight smile. “Why else do you think I suggested the airport? It’s not like I like to hang out here.”<br>“How were we supposed to know?” Daemon responded, eyeing the manhole like it was the last thing he wanted to climb into. Ditto. “You’re an Arum, so . . .”<br>“I really was hoping you’d drop that damn attitude by now.”<br>Daemon smirked. “Kiss my ass.”<br>“No, thank you.”</b>
</i><br><br>Oh, I almost forgot the cherries on the top. Lotho, you're crazy, but I like you. Nancy Husher, Sadi and Ethan Smith -- eff you all.<br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NxE8C7Rl9ok/U-NOeH6aZmI/AAAAAAAAOHU/hdP1Knii3tI/s1600/tumblr_n16smoWr2V1tqzyg1o1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709637.gif" height="162" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Prepare yourself for action, battles and a colossal amount of ass-kicking. To say that Daemon &amp; Co. are badass would be an understatement. This little enlarged family became a team that supported each other, sacrificed for one another and protected everyone at any cost. Honestly, I felt like a proud mamma to see those babies take on the world with their eyes set on a future. They’re determined, selfless and down-right awesome. <br><br><i>
  <b>“Luxen, by nature, are arrogant.”<br>“Gee, really?” I muttered.<br>One side of his lips kicked up in a sexy, smug half grin as Archer snickered.<br>“Origins are probably more arrogant, you know,” Daemon said. “The borderline stupid kind of arrogant.”<br>The smirk faded from Archer’s face.”</b>
</i><br><br>But there’s also heartbreak in store for them so you might shed a few tears. There was a certain moment when my eyes glazed over, got all teary-eyed and made me shake my head in vehement denial. The scene did stupid, cruel things to my heart and it opened the floodgates, as I was about to go shouting to the whole world that <b>“LIFE IS FREAKING UNFAIR!”</b>. That part, short-lived as it was, pretty much crushed me.<br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-poDaHrOSFX8/U-NOXsoiapI/AAAAAAAAOGU/_8Arm8-nXeE/s1600/39875-Emma-Stone-no-no-no-no-no-gif-bGod.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709638.gif" height="145" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then there’s the epilogue that had my cheeks hurting from smiling so much and my heart completely satisfied. I was doing a happy dance at how things played out, because these beloved characters of mine got the ending they deserved after hard and gut-wrenching experiences. I was so so proud and happy for them. <i>*sniff*</i><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-AWvl1Mw_frY/U-NOaAcZWFI/AAAAAAAAOGw/lo-Xp4z6ErI/s1600/giphy.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709639.gif" height="180" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And I’ll miss them so damn much. <i>*full on sobbing*</i><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-_yDhlu5v84s/U-NOYyMY13I/AAAAAAAAOGc/uhj9JOtuMEI/s1600/10341878.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709640.gif" height="187" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So here we are, at the end of another astounding series. In this last installment, I fell all over again for the awesomeness that is Daemon Black, cheered Katy as she evolved into this kick-ass young woman, devoured every word about the rest of the crew, laughed my ass off uncountable times and had my heart leaping from my chest at every threat. <i>Opposition</i> was well worth the wait and the jazz went down in pure JLA fashion – truly unputdownable, swoon-worthy, hilarious and action-packed. If you’re afraid to read it, have no fear – it’s glorious. If you haven’t started this series yet, then I seriously don’t know what the hell are you waiting for.<br><br><i>
  <b>“This kind of love was the real deal, stronger than a whole planet full of psycho aliens and an entire government.”</b>
</i><br><br>Oh, man. I guess there’s one last thing that needs to be said…<br><br>Thank you, Jennifer, for <b>creating one of the best stories out there.</b><br>Thank you, Jennifer, for <b>allowing us to embark on this journey.</b><br>Thank you, Jennifer, for <b>making me fall in love with your incredible and amazing characters.</b><br>Thank you, Jennifer, for <b>making me cry, laugh out loud, swoon off my feet, smile from ear to ear and cheer.</b><br>Thank you, thank you, thank <i>you</i>. It has been wonderful from start to finish.<br><br><b>ENJOY! &lt;3<br><br>P.S.</b> Basically Archer to Daemon &amp; Katy:<br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-TDqAOhAMeNo/U-NOeTD2U-I/AAAAAAAAOHY/fFXyROfzLXk/s1600/tumblr_n8kp4khYYo1ruu897o2_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407405946ra/10709641.gif" height="143" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>BEFORE READING: HOLY BABY ORIGINS!</b><br><br>I'm already having Daemon Black withdrawals. I thought the ending of <i>Opal</i> was bad, but <i>Origin</i> managed to end in a jaw-dropping way. I'm mind-blown. <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-F2udo78xZoo/Uh3agRoHfZI/AAAAAAAAMY8/yPquiOSKDrQ/s1600/tumblr_inline_mocoyzHE0b1qz4rgp.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384908ra/743604.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I WANT <i>Opposition</i> like yesterday! (By the way, awesome title.)<br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kEvUIZOR6W4/Uh3Zujhpa-I/AAAAAAAAMYk/bGzGdagx-6k/s1600/BloomGimme.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="149" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384908ra/743605.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I NEED to know what happens now! This whole thing is so much bigger than Daemon &amp; Co.!<br><br><b>HOW CAN I WAIT ANOTHER YEAR???? <br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1CNYSOHrq70/Uh3aPk-TdUI/AAAAAAAAMY0/LgQCukQ1lNc/s1600/tumblr_inline_mgny4ynxVO1r29lcx.gif" rel="nofollow noopener"><img height="179" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384908ra/743606.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>HOOOOOOOW?!?!</b><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-InUGw2g7KRE/Uh3aMZ8F5iI/AAAAAAAAMYs/YdszpQ0dZto/s1600/tumblr_m5ojmo2U6Z1rvtuxmo1_250.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384908ra/743607.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And now I'm positive JLA is an evil woman. <br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7urpA6-jPQw/Uh3dRlCZ0PI/AAAAAAAAMZU/izQ8TqhsB-4/s1600/tumblr_inline_moyd1zId7R1qz4rgp.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384908ra/743608.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>Hmph.</b>
</i> </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10379627600730666115"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"You ready to play, Kitten?"</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407331809i/10676091._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='271' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>Opposition</i> was bittersweet for me, it's the final book in the Lux series. The world is in chaos, between fighting invading aliens and secret government agencies - is there a light at the end of the tunnel for Daemon and Katy?<br/><br/><b>
  <i>I knew in that tiny second as we stared each other down that this was the beginning and this was also the end. The Luxen were truly invading.</i>
</b><br/> <br/>Katy was such a badass in this book, and of course Daemon had me constantly swooning. I</span>
  <span id="freeText10379627600730666115" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><i>
  <b>"You ready to play, Kitten?"</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407331809i/10676091._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="271" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Opposition</i> was bittersweet for me, it's the final book in the Lux series. The world is in chaos, between fighting invading aliens and secret government agencies - is there a light at the end of the tunnel for Daemon and Katy?<br><br><b>
  <i>I knew in that tiny second as we stared each other down that this was the beginning and this was also the end. The Luxen were truly invading.</i>
</b><br> <br>Katy was such a badass in this book, and of course Daemon had me constantly swooning. I really enjoyed this action-packed conclusion, but it did seem to end quickly. I guess I will always want more. I will miss these characters, the banter, the friendship and the love - it's been an awesome journey. And I really wish Archer would get a book, love him &lt;33<br><br><i>
  <b>"I think you do like Archer, and you just don’t want to admit that you’re in the beginning stages of a bromance to end all bromances."</b>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1766070915" />
    <a title="DW" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40762852-dw"><img alt="DW" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536259397p2/40762852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1766070915?book_show_action=true">Sep 24, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="DW" class="user" itemprop="url" name="DW" href="/user/show/40762852-dw">DW</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40762852-dw?shelf=lux">lux</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1766070915" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4638937676329453005"><b>Holy Alien butt cracks, that was frigging fantastic!!!<br/><br/><br/>The entire Lux series has been five stars for me. I don't think that there was anything about these books that I did not like. <br/><br/><a href='http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/C834A01A-FCD7-49A9-B398-87E0D5572D20_zpscivmrpbw.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474760138i/20638957.jpg' alt=' photo C834A01A-FCD7-49A9-B398-87E0D5572D20_zpscivmrpbw.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><i><b>"I broke every rule of my kind to heal you and keep you with me. I married you and burned down an entire city to keep you safe. I’ve killed for you. Did you think I’d forget what you mean to me? That anything in this world—in any world—would be stronger than my love for you?”<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/769A7274-4C3C-43AA-A742-64BE2D0C7FEF_zpsfkefoh9f.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474760138i/20638958.png' alt=' photo 769A7274-4C3C-43AA-A742-64BE2D0C7FEF_zpsfkefoh9f.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Daemon Black is sexy, arrogant, kicks ass a</b></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText4638937676329453005" style="display:none"><b>Holy Alien butt cracks, that was frigging fantastic!!!<br><br><br>The entire Lux series has been five stars for me. I don't think that there was anything about these books that I did not like. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/C834A01A-FCD7-49A9-B398-87E0D5572D20_zpscivmrpbw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474760138i/20638957.jpg" alt=" photo C834A01A-FCD7-49A9-B398-87E0D5572D20_zpscivmrpbw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><i><b>"I broke every rule of my kind to heal you and keep you with me. I married you and burned down an entire city to keep you safe. I’ve killed for you. Did you think I’d forget what you mean to me? That anything in this world—in any world—would be stronger than my love for you?”<br><br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/769A7274-4C3C-43AA-A742-64BE2D0C7FEF_zpsfkefoh9f.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474760138i/20638958.png" alt=" photo 769A7274-4C3C-43AA-A742-64BE2D0C7FEF_zpsfkefoh9f.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Daemon Black is sexy, arrogant, kicks ass and protects the ones that he loves especially Katy. There is absolutely nothing that he wouldn't do for her. He would burn the world down and fight his own kind to protect Katy. That is exactly what he did. From the very first book, I knew that I was going to love Daemon even if at times I wanted to punch him in the face. His arrogance was a little over the top in the beginning but like he said:<br><br><br> "Luxen are naturally arrogant"<br><br><br>By the second book I was pretty much in love with this gorgeous alien. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/B809D2DE-EC3C-4FB0-A747-C65394A19F50_zpsxxhznjhi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474760138i/20638959.jpg" alt=" photo B809D2DE-EC3C-4FB0-A747-C65394A19F50_zpsxxhznjhi.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>Katy was badass. I mean she fought just as hard as everyone else. Her love for Daemon would not let her fail when she was fighting the Arum, Luxen or the Origins. I loved her personality so much and the fact that she didn't let Daemon tell her what to do just made me love her even more. <br><br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/E862D947-151F-4A8D-9C4F-C57E19EA5B99_zps9zphnakh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474760138i/20638960._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo E862D947-151F-4A8D-9C4F-C57E19EA5B99_zps9zphnakh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>I liked the secondary characters with the exception of Andrew and Ash. I was so not a fan of theirs. Dawson, Dee, Adam, Archer and even Luc were great though. <br><br><br>Sooo... If you are a fan of aliens, action and some romance, then you might really like this series. I know that I sure did!</b></i></b></span>
