        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/474294388?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie Monroe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie Monroe" href="/user/show/6688207-natalie-monroe">Natalie Monroe</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=cheesy-cheesy-cheesy">cheesy-cheesy-cheesy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=kick-ass-heroines">kick-ass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=not-as-good-as-i-expected">not-as-good-as-i-expected</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=good-but-not-great">good-but-not-great</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=awesome-author">awesome-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=pants-are-snowmen-and-they-are-june">pants-are-snowmen-and-they-are-june</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer474294388" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16215258226637651693"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/> <br/><blockquote>
  <i>“Kat whipped toward me, her eyes glowing from within. In that moment, she looked like a goddess—a goddess of vengeance.<br/><br/>[Daemon's thoughts:] If we weren’t in the middle of a fight, I’d have you up against a tree right now.” </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>If I had to compare this finale to food, it would be porridge. It's satisfying, fills your stomach and you can even mix in honey or raisins to sweeten it. But you wouldn't ask for seconds. Not to mention three very angry bears that would be on you faster than you</span>
  <span id="freeText16215258226637651693" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>“Kat whipped toward me, her eyes glowing from within. In that moment, she looked like a goddess—a goddess of vengeance.<br><br>[Daemon's thoughts:] If we weren’t in the middle of a fight, I’d have you up against a tree right now.” </i>
</blockquote><br><br>If I had to compare this finale to food, it would be porridge. It's satisfying, fills your stomach and you can even mix in honey or raisins to sweeten it. But you wouldn't ask for seconds. Not to mention three very angry bears that would be on you faster than you can say, "Goldilocks did it!"<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416228924ra/11915031.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Gimme back my porridge!<br><br><b>Here's a basic rundown of the plot:</b><br><br>Katy: I miss Daemon and his green eyes. Oh, and aliens have invaded our planet.<br><br>Bethany: I'm <s>sixteen and</s> pregnant.<br><br>Katy: OMG, she's going to have a <s>vampire</s> alien hybrid baby!!<br><br>Luc and Archer: Lol, we knew all along.<br><br>Katy: SHE HAS TO HAVE PRENATAL VITAMINS!<br><br>Luc and Archer: It's really dangerous out there.<br><br>Katy: SHE HAS TO HAVE PRENATAL VITAMINS!<br><br>Luc and Archer: Lol, okay.<br><br>Katy: OMG, there are aliens in the supermarket! And a dude with green eyes! *blacks out*<br><br>Dawson: Lol, I may have just paralyzed my sister-in-law with my alien powers. Ooh, level 69 of Candy Crush.<br><br>Daemon: I hate this redheaded chick that keeps throwing herself at me. I am immune to freaky alien hive mentality because of true love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416228924i/11915032.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dee: I AM NOW EVIL BECAUSE I DO NOT HAVE TRUE LOVE. *sad face*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416228924ra/11915033.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Katy: OMG, Dee is evil now! And Daemon is mean! <br><br>Daemon: I only did that to protect you. Now come here, sweetcheeks.<br><br>Katy: Ugh, redheaded chick is such a slut. I know this because she is pretty.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416228924ra/11915034.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Explosions! Excitement!</u><br><br>Daemon: Wow, that was close. Wanna have sex?<br><br>Katy: Lol, okay.<br><br>Archer: I'm back if anyone cares.<br><br>Daemon: I hate Archer because he hugged Katy longer than the three-second rule. Wanna have sex, Katy?<br><br>Katy: Lol, okay.<br><br>Random government official: I AM GOING DESTROY A FEW STATES TO SAVE HUMANKIND.<br><br>Katy, OMG, you can't do that! Innocents will die!<br><br>Random government official: THEN WHAT DO YOU SUGGEST?<br><br>Katy: ...The Avengers.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416228924ra/11915035.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Daemon: I know! Let's use the Secret Weapon.<br><br>Katy: OMG, that's perfect!<br><br>Daemon: I know I am. Wanna have sex?<br><br>Katy: Lol, okay.<br><br><u>Road trip!</u><br><br>Daemon: Wanna have shower sex?<br><br>Katy: Lol, okay.<br><br>Secret Weapon: I want to have non-penetrative sex with your girlfriend because I enjoy being arbitrary.<br><br>Katy: Ew! But okay.<br><br>Daemon: Absolutely not! Testosterone level rising...<br><br>Katy: I must use my non-virgin flesh for the good of humankind.<br><br>Secret Weapon: Haha, you noobs were really going to go through with it! Okay, I'll help you because I enjoy being arbitrary.<br><br>Daemon: Whew, that was close! Wanna have sex?<br><br>Katy: Lol, okay.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381132416ra/4320834.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Sense a pattern? <br><br>The above makes it seem like I hated Opposition, but I honestly enjoyed it. It's readable, as with all Armentrout's work, has a logical plot that links up with earlier installments and a competent heroine that kicks butt. There's a female friendship scene that could've walked straight out of Frozen <i>and</i> lots of sex. <br><br>Too much sex, but that's another matter. <br><br>All too often, YA authors have their characters do the dirty once, usually without a condom I may add, and never have them make love again. It comes off as a grandiose display of their never-ending love for each other rather than a normal activity that real-life couples engage in when they're ready. Not Katy and Daemon. They hump like bunnies. Who have access to condoms.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“It's like you have a special skill when it comes to finding condoms. Seriously. They must fall out of the sky whenever you're around.” </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416157557ra/11904109.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But as a person who loved the first three volumes, which were straight-up paranormal romance, this installment pales in comparison. There's an equal distribution between romance and plot, but when you chase two rabbits at once, you're bound to disappoint someone. I vote for more plot; those kids need to have a tighter grasp on their hormones during the apocalypse.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416228924ra/11915036.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I may rate this book higher in retrospect after I read the whole series in one go, but for now, 3.5 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16215258226637651693" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer12642911215536368605"><b>
  <i>“Did you think I’d forget what you mean to me? That anything in this world—in any world—would be stronger than my love for you?”</i>
</b><br/><br/>*screams in the distance<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528247060ra/25665763.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><p>
  <u>Nothing can get in the way of Daemon and Kath.</u>
</p><br/>The amount of development, love and passion they have is superb! <br/>I’m crying at how incredible their love is. <br/>One of the main reasons why I loved this series so much. <br/>I just love the dynamic they have, and every time they have a scene together I could feel the love and my heart just burst with </span>
  <span id="freeText12642911215536368605" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“Did you think I’d forget what you mean to me? That anything in this world—in any world—would be stronger than my love for you?”</i>
</b><br><br>*screams in the distance<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528247060ra/25665763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><p>
  <u>Nothing can get in the way of Daemon and Kath.</u>
</p><br>The amount of development, love and passion they have is superb! <br>I’m crying at how incredible their love is. <br>One of the main reasons why I loved this series so much. <br>I just love the dynamic they have, and every time they have a scene together I could feel the love and my heart just burst with so much happiness and I wanted to cry because they are so perfect.<br><br>The start of the book got me a bit confused but then everything made sense and I just got so into the story I honestly don’t know what to do now that I’m done.<br>That’s the problem of reading the last 3 books in last then a week, I honestly have to learn how to savour the books and read slower so I don’t have to say goodbye so fast to amazing fantastic characters that I’m going to miss very much.<br><br>I love all of the side characters so much, Dee, Luc, Archer..... and so on. They are so cool and awesome and badass. I’m happy I got to see more of them. <br>Oh, and Archer and Daemon are just the BROMANCE I didn’t know I need it. *lol<br><br><br>A lot of things that happened I wasn’t expecting and damn I was shocked.<br>In the first 2 books, the only thing I care about was Daemon and Kath’s relationship but has the series progressed I started to enjoy the world and everything else that these books bring and I’m happy I did.<br><br><br>I’M SO HAPPY THIS WASN’T A SHITTING ENDING. Witch, I was a bit surprised considering that most series have, well, a not very good ending. This one was the opposite, it had a fantastic end, and I could imagine a better one.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528247061ra/25665764.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But at the same time, I’m sad because IS OVER. (goodbye Daemon my dear adorable beautiful man! I’m going to miss you the most).<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528247061ra/25665765.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(I hate that when I look for a sad supernatural gif, Dean is all that appears, FML).<br><br><br>FAREWELL Lux series! Bye, my babies. My OTP f.o.r.e.v.e.r I’ll reread you in the near future. ❤️</span>

<div id="review_414721763" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/414721763" />
    <a title="Tina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6383594-tina"><img alt="Tina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371867364p2/6383594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/414721763?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tina" href="/user/show/6383594-tina">Tina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer414721763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11787594378733857280">4.5 Stars!<br/><br/>AMAZING. AMAZING AMAZING AMAZING! AH-MAY-ZING! I’m biased (just to let you know) when I say that this book was a fantastic end to a wonderful series! I’ve been a huge Lux fan since book 1 (as well as an Armentrout fan overall) and still am so it’s no surprised that I found this book absolutely wonderful. Like Ms. Armentrout, I too find it bittersweet to see this series end. I’ll keep this review brief-ish since I’m never really good at writing reviews for the last book in a series.<br/><br/>This</span>
  <span id="freeText11787594378733857280" style="display:none">4.5 Stars!<br /><br />AMAZING. AMAZING AMAZING AMAZING! AH-MAY-ZING! I’m biased (just to let you know) when I say that this book was a fantastic end to a wonderful series! I’ve been a huge Lux fan since book 1 (as well as an Armentrout fan overall) and still am so it’s no surprised that I found this book absolutely wonderful. Like Ms. Armentrout, I too find it bittersweet to see this series end. I’ll keep this review brief-ish since I’m never really good at writing reviews for the last book in a series.<br /><br />This book finished the series off strong and nice.The book starts off not too long after the ending of the previous book so technically a lot of time hasn’t passed, but a lot did happen (at least on Daemon, Dee, and Dawson’s side). From there, the entire book is an emotional roller coaster ride as there’s confusion about why this person’s doing this, who’s on which side, immediate frustration with characters whom you wish you could kick in their appropriate gender genitals, and sweet, sexy romance.<br /><br />If there’s one thing I can guarantee you, it’s that the writing is just as good (if not better) than her previous books in the Lux series. You the familiar dialogue between characters as well as the familiar humor you know and love like twerking being essential in help saving the day.<br />I kid you not, twerking (in some shape/form), helped Kat get out of a tight pickle in the first quarter of the book.<br /><br />As for the romance and sexy time, Ms. Armentrout makes a good balance between action and romance. She includes enough romance where emotional progress is evidently made while also making sure that it doesn’t completely overshadow the main problem at hand. Now whether that romance is really progression or regression, I won’t say so I don’t spoil it for all y’all who haven’t read/finished reading it yet ;)<br /><br /><br />Overall, the story was fantastic! I have very few and very minor gripes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[like the resolution with Ethan and Nancy being over a little too fast as well as a slightly easy way out with the rest of the Luxen <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but, again, I was happy overall with the end result. I’m absolutely sad to see this series over, but, as they say, all good things must come to an end. Thank you Ms. Armentrout for a wonderful series and characters! I absolutely can’t wait for any new series you may have in the future!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11787594378733857280" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/710517553" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/710517553?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer710517553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2566239600941321215"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/luxseries_zpsd0aafe42.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407504197i/10730860.jpg' alt=' photo luxseries_zpsd0aafe42.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Opposition is book number five in the Lux series by Jennifer L. Armentrout. How in the world do I ever do this book or this series justice in a review? I have loved this series from page one of book one. It’s a wonder my heart survived all the action scenes and will any other book couple ever be able to compete with Daemon and Katy? No, I don’t think so. Even though I am saddened to say goodbye to these characters, JLA did a fantastic job in this series conclusion. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I wasn’t the same girl</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText2566239600941321215" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/luxseries_zpsd0aafe42.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407504197i/10730860.jpg" alt=" photo luxseries_zpsd0aafe42.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Opposition is book number five in the Lux series by Jennifer L. Armentrout. How in the world do I ever do this book or this series justice in a review? I have loved this series from page one of book one. It’s a wonder my heart survived all the action scenes and will any other book couple ever be able to compete with Daemon and Katy? No, I don’t think so. Even though I am saddened to say goodbye to these characters, JLA did a fantastic job in this series conclusion. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I wasn’t the same girl who had knocked on Daemon’s door, I would probably never be that girl again.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mtglefmFX41sr4mfco1_500_zps01593482.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407504197ra/10730861.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mtglefmFX41sr4mfco1_500_zps01593482.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We start right up where the previous book ended, The Luxen have arrived. She, Beth, Archer and Luc are waiting in the cabin for Dee, Dawson and Daemon to return. But they don’t show up. Why haven’t they come back? Where are they? And Katy finds out what everyone else already knew, Beth is pregnant. But, she isn’t doing well at all. There are things she needs, so Katy and Archer head out to the supermarket to pick up some things…maybe not the best decision. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ob_zps4f7e0281.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407504197i/10730862.jpg" alt=" photo ob_zps4f7e0281.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Yes, the Luxen are here. There are thousands of them, maybe even millions. They are killing the humans and have learned to assimilate the DNA from a human to take their form. What do they want? To take over the world? And who is in charge? Cities are being destroyed and so many lives are lost. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Daemon was okay. He was himself, and dammit, together we could face anything. We would because we had to.”</i>
</b><br><br>Daemon and Katy face the biggest challenge of all, to stop the Luxen from taking over earth. It is a war, and they don’t know who to trust. Old enemies now become allies. I do want to say that Hunter, the Arum from Obsession, is brought back in this book. For me this was a dream come true. To have them both on the same page, well, it was almost more than I could handle. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ja_zps0fc32623.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407504197i/10730863.jpg" alt=" photo ja_zps0fc32623.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"God, I loved Daemon. I was in love with him as much as I had been the very first time I recognized what that burning sensation was, what that almost electric shock every time we touched meant. This kind of love was the real deal, stronger than a whole planet full of psycho aliens and an entire government.”</i>
</b> <br><br>We meet a new character in this book, Lotho, the leader of the Arum. He was crazy, psychotic and hilarious. It seems like the Arum could have their own series. I love, love, love Hunter. I am dropping a hint here Ms. Armentrout. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n51ngm9VX91syb3aio4_250_zps25070883.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407504197ra/10730864.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n51ngm9VX91syb3aio4_250_zps25070883.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Daemon kissed like he was staking a claim, but he already had me—all of me. My heart. My soul. My whole being.”</i>
</b><br><br>This book is a highlighter’s dream. I had such a hard time choosing which quotes to include. The things Daemon says to Katy, well, all I can do is “sigh.” This book will make you laugh plenty of times, cry, and sigh (a lot.) And I think there is a moral to the story. For me, I think it is the old adage, “love conquers all.” The power of the love between Daemon and Katy, and even Dawson and Beth, is what saved them all. So, if you have been considering starting this series, I say, “What the heck are you waiting for?” You are in for the ride of your life. Jennifer Armentrout, all I can say is thank you. I tried to think of something deeper, something more memorable but all I can come up with is, “Thank you!”<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’ve got a big heart, Kitten.” His lips cruised over mine as he spoke. “That’s what I love about you most. Well, that and I am a really big fan of your sweet body, but your heart? Yeah, that completes the package of you, wraps it up with a nice little bow. It makes you perfect to me.”</i>
</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mwtseeAGmn1t0i1e4o1_500_zps8e6f775a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407504197ra/10730865.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mwtseeAGmn1t0i1e4o1_500_zps8e6f775a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2566239600941321215" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_712974083" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/712974083" />
    <a title="Aimz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17001482-aimz"><img alt="Aimz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1496015385p2/17001482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/712974083?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aimz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aimz" href="/user/show/17001482-aimz">Aimz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1753760574972876980">OMG I don't even know where to start. I put off reading this for a week. I wasn't ready for the end. I knew it would break my heart to say goodbye. I fell so hard for this series. And it was a long year to get to this beautiful ending. Thank you Ms Armentrout. Thank you for giving this story life. Thank you for sharing so much of yourself for our simple entertainment. Reading saves all of us in different ways. This series saved me last year when I was in a bad place. It brought me out of a hole.</span>
  <span id="freeText1753760574972876980" style="display:none">OMG I don't even know where to start. I put off reading this for a week. I wasn't ready for the end. I knew it would break my heart to say goodbye. I fell so hard for this series. And it was a long year to get to this beautiful ending. Thank you Ms Armentrout. Thank you for giving this story life. Thank you for sharing so much of yourself for our simple entertainment. Reading saves all of us in different ways. This series saved me last year when I was in a bad place. It brought me out of a hole. So thank you Katy and Daemon. Five stars doesn't seem like enough.</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('D9fa6Wqn+ZRpTeV1vmI72HFJSxKG98R7Wofu/VnMtbs18bM70fkw/M5mURRJlzEHpxas2kh6ShwB+ahMlI9HIQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PwivLegAZcJVmcyLOMJltwhXABax2/0FD1BZqHkEqlgFLsb/U16sqvKyeOrPN29o3gjn3n9Wc2JULh8ZtEdYwg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText8652297835425248406" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>

        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }
  if (w.attachEvent) {
    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>
